My sister-in-law scheduled an appointment for my Mom at 1:00 p.m. on July 28, 2018. I arrived with my Mom 15 minutes early. We were told by the owner that there was a 20 minute wait. My Mom was not seated until 1:20 p.m.

There was another woman who came in about 15 minutes after our arrival and she was seated at the same time my Mom was, no waiting for her and her pedicure was started   before my Mother's pedicure.

< text>
Public Storage is a scam. They get you in the door with a low initial rate, and then raise their prices after you're already moved in. BEWARE! I've watched them raise our rates 3 times now and we're paying almost 50% more than the original price offered. Our exact same unit is being offered for half the price to new customers. Now we are stuck and it seems extremely unethical that Public Storage exploits its customers in this way. When I call they say their costs went up this year!? Inflation was not 50% and Public Storage's costs have not gone up by 50%, so the increases are pure profit going to their business because they are exploiting customers who cant immediately haul everything they have stored. BEWARE! Do not store your items with Public Storage more than 6 months unless you are ready to pay huge rate increases. < Text>
All other Quality Inns I've stayed in looked well decorated, fresh and inviting, and made me happy upon walking in the door. < review>
Such a great place to grab British food - vast array of confectionery choices and some good stuff to take home - like a sausages rolls and what not!</review>

<userid>106542597949448755915< /userid><Date>1622322850990< /Date></record></dataset><record>
<userid>114540592151182960985<//userid><Name>Joy< /Name>< time>
1599685448275<//time>
< rate>
5< /rate>
< review>
I visited in June and the experience was quite wonderful. I love tea but the people I came with don't drink it much. Our waitress spent the time to explain the different teas on their menu and provided some recommendations.

I love the personalized tea set each person gets! One tea pot is plenty for yourself. As for the food accompaniments, I love the variety of the finger sandwiches. By the time we got to the bottom tier we were quite stuffed from it.

They also have a gift shop where they sell the tea blends they serve. I happily came home with a bag of their creme caramel rooibos tea leaves. I can't wait to visit again!< /review>

< Review>
I made a reservation here for two for Christmas Afternoon Tea. I thought it was nice that they gave a courtesy call the day before to remind me of the reservation.

At $30 per person, the price is steeper than what we typically spend on lunch, but my friend and I thought it was good to treat ourselves once in a while. I liked that there were lots of non-American candies and chocolates to browse inside the shop and we really liked the tea station set up for us to sample each blend before making our decisions for the tea.

The patio the tea is served in is quite small and a little crowded, and there isn't really a place to put larger purses. The food overall was okay. My friend and I weren't particularly blown away by it: the bread for the sandwiches were on the dry side, and we both found the sausage rolls and yorkshire pudding to be too salty, scone and cream were heavy, and we weren't quite sure what to make of the strawberry rhubarb crumble and the mince pie. But I do realize these are differences in personal preferences (aside from the dry bread, but reading other reviews it appears this is a regular thing here) and I could see why people like the food, it just wasn't for us. My friend and I really liked their strawberry jam and their port wine syllabub, though! And the teas were great. I'd recommend the cream tea instead of the full spread for people with smaller appetites who wanna try this place for the experience.

I'd probably give this tea room a solid 3/5 solely for the food but added a star since the tea and service were good and my friend and I still thought this was a good experience to try out. I might come back in the future to try a new tea blend and different monthly menu.< /Review>

UPDATE: my sister did call and speak with a person who confirmed that it was safe for celiacs which is why we came in. I appreciate the attention to this matter (we got an email from the owner) as having celiacs is a much more dangerous condition than a gluten sensitivity. It is not uncommon for restaurants to label food as gluten free but with an asterisks (cross contamination is possible). I personally cannot eat at those places. I just didn’t want another celiac customer to suffer the same fate. My sister loves this shop and has always brought friends, the service was fine, the rest of the evening was no fun!

Attention those with celiacs or gluten sensitivity. This store promised their gluten free menu was safe for all but it was not. We went for gluten free tea service and I spent the rest of the night sick to my stomach (I’ll omit the details). The tea service was fine, but when we called to report that there was an obvious contamination, they were unapologetic. We have left messages with the owner and have not heard back at this time. We wanted to ensure that they didn’t guarantee a gluten free experience without possibility of contamination. So if you are sensitive like me, skip it!<//Review>

<date>1487016489558</date>< Text>
(Translated by Google) I love the place. The trouble is that it has become very popular and it is difficult to get reservations for the High Noon Tea on the weekend. But if you can go on weekdays or make reservations in advance, I really recommend them. The service is good, the price may sound high, but the truth is a complete meal and worth it.
When you subscribe to the newsletter you receive invitations to the Wednesday of tea that are thematic, fun and enjoyable.
If they are not teas, they should go to the store anyway, it has many British foods and items (I found a delicious assam).

(Original)
Me encanta el lugar. Lo malo es que se ha vuelto muy popular y es difícil conseguir reservaciones para el High Noon Tea en fin de semana. Pero si pueden ir entre semana o hacer reservaciones con tiempo, la verdad se los recomiendo ampliamente. El servicio es bueno,  el precio puede sonar alto, pero la verdad es una comida completa y vale la pena.
Al subscribirse al newsletter les llegan invitaciones a los miércoles de té que son temáticos, son divertidos y amenos.
Si no son de tés, de todos modos deben ir a la tienda, tiene muchos alimentos y artículos británicos (encontre un assam delicioso).< /Text>
